                   mGeneralLedgerSetup.GET();
                   mGeneralLedgerSetup.TESTFIELD("LCY Code");
                   mCompanyInformation.GET();
                   mCompanyInformation.CALCFIELDS(Picture);
                   DetectLogInteraction();

    OnPreReport=BEGIN
                  InitialiseRequestPageData();
                  VerifyDates();
                  CalculateAgingBandDates();
                  InitialiseCurrencies();
                  mFormatAddress.Company(mCompanyAddress, mCompanyInformation);

                  mSalesPrintoutToolkit.CompanyShortAddress(mCompanyShortAddress);
                  mSalesPrintoutToolkit.ReportImages(mFooterImage, TRUE);
                END;

    PreviewMode=PrintLayout;

               DataItemTable=Table18;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(No.);

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF ( NOT (DecideWhetherToIncludeCustomer())) THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP();

                                  mAgingBandBufferTmp.RESET();

                                  CurrReport.PAGENO := 1;
                                  CurrReport.LANGUAGE := mLanguage.GetLanguageID("Language Code");

                                  mFormatAddress.Customer(mCustomerAddress, dCustomer);

                                  UpdateLastStatementNo();
                                  LogInteraction();

                                  mReportTitle := STRSUBSTNO(tReportTitle, dCustomer."Last Statement No.");
                                  mReportSubtitle := STRSUBSTNO(tReportSubtitle, dCustomer.Name, dCustomer."No.");
                                  mReportDates := STRSUBSTNO(tReportDates, FORMAT(mStartDate, 0, 1), FORMAT(mEndDate, 0, 1));

                                  dCustomer.SETRANGE("Date Filter", mStartDate, mEndDate);
                                  dCustomer.CALCFIELDS("Balance (LCY)");
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=No.,Search Name,Print Statements,Currency Filter }

    { 6523;1   ;DataItem;dEntryCurrency      ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 WHERE(Number=FILTER(1..));
               PrintOnlyIfDetail=Yes;
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               mCurrencyTmp.RESET();
                               IF (dCustomer.GETFILTER("Currency Filter") <> '') THEN
                                 dCustomer.COPYFILTER("Currency Filter", mCurrencyTmp.Code);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  lContinue@1000000000 : Boolean;
                                BEGIN
                                  lContinue := FALSE;
                                  IF (dEntryCurrency.Number = 1) THEN
                                    lContinue := mCurrencyTmp.FINDSET()
                                  ELSE
                                    lContinue := (mCurrencyTmp.NEXT <> 0);
                                  IF ( NOT (lContinue)) THEN
                                    CurrReport.BREAK();

                                  mCustLedgerEntry.RESET();
                                  mCustLedgerEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Customer No.", "Posting Date", "Currency Code");
                                  mCustLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Customer No.", dCustomer."No.");
                                  mCustLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Posting Date", 0D, mEndDate);
                                  mCustLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Currency Code", mCurrencyTmp.Code);
                                  IF (mCustLedgerEntry.ISEMPTY) THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP();

                                  mCustomer := dCustomer;
                                  mCustomer.SETRANGE("Date Filter", 0D, mStartDate - 1);
                                   mCustomer.SETRANGE("Currency Filter",mCurrencyTmp.Code);
                                  mCustomer.CALCFIELDS("Net Change");
                                  mEntryCurrencyStartBalance := mCustomer."Net Change";
                                  mEntryBalanceAmount := mCustomer."Net Change";
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1000000055;2;Column;Indicator_EC       ;

    { 9366;2   ;DataItem;dEntry              ;
               DataItemTable=Table379;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Customer No.,Posting Date,Entry Type,Currency Code);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               dEntry.SETRANGE("Customer No.", dCustomer."No.");
                               dEntry.SETRANGE("Posting Date", mStartDate, mEndDate);
                               dEntry.SETRANGE("Currency Code", mCurrencyTmp.Code);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  lIncludeEntry@1000000000 : Boolean;
                                BEGIN
                                  IF ((SkipReversedUnapplied(dEntry)) OR (dEntry.Amount = 0)) THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP();

                                  CLEAR(mEntryDescription);
                                  CLEAR(mEntryDueDate);
                                  CLEAR(mEntryRemainingAmount);

                                  lIncludeEntry := TRUE;
                                  CASE (dEntry."Entry Type") OF
                                    dEntry."Entry Type"::"Initial Entry":
                                      BEGIN
                                        mCustLedgerEntry.GET(dEntry."Cust. Ledger Entry No.");
                                        mEntryDescription := mCustLedgerEntry.Description;
                                        mEntryDueDate := mCustLedgerEntry."Due Date";
                                        mCustLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Date Filter", 0D, mEndDate);
                                        mCustLedgerEntry.CALCFIELDS("Remaining Amount");
                                        mEntryRemainingAmount := mCustLedgerEntry."Remaining Amount";
                                        mCustLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Date Filter");
                                      END;
                                    dEntry."Entry Type"::Application:
                                      BEGIN
                                        mDetailedCustLedgEntry.RESET();
                                        mDetailedCustLedgEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Customer No.", "Posting Date", "Entry Type");
                                        mDetailedCustLedgEntry.SETRANGE("Customer No.", dEntry."Customer No.");
                                        mDetailedCustLedgEntry.SETRANGE("Posting Date", dEntry."Posting Date");
                                        mDetailedCustLedgEntry.SETRANGE("Entry Type", dEntry."Entry Type"::Application);
                                        mDetailedCustLedgEntry.SETRANGE("Transaction No.", dEntry."Transaction No.");
                                        mDetailedCustLedgEntry.SETFILTER("Currency Code", '<>%1', dEntry."Currency Code");
                                        IF ( NOT (mDetailedCustLedgEntry.ISEMPTY)) THEN
                                        BEGIN
                                          mEntryDescription := tMulticurrencyApplication;
                                          mEntryDueDate := 0D;
                                        END
                                        ELSE
                                          lIncludeEntry := FALSE;
                                      END;
                                    dEntry."Entry Type"::"Payment Discount",
                                    dEntry."Entry Type"::"Payment Discount (VAT Excl.)",
                                    dEntry."Entry Type"::"Payment Discount (VAT Adjustment)",
                                    dEntry."Entry Type"::"Payment Discount Tolerance",
                                    dEntry."Entry Type"::"Payment Discount Tolerance (VAT Excl.)",
                                    dEntry."Entry Type"::"Payment Discount Tolerance (VAT Adjustment)":
                                      BEGIN
                                        mEntryDescription := tPaymentDiscount;
                                        mEntryDueDate := 0D;
                                      END;
                                    dEntry."Entry Type"::"Payment Tolerance",
                                    dEntry."Entry Type"::"Payment Tolerance (VAT Excl.)",
                                    dEntry."Entry Type"::"Payment Tolerance (VAT Adjustment)":
                                      BEGIN
                                        mEntryDescription := tApplicationWriteoffs;
                                        mEntryDueDate := 0D;
                                      END;
                                    dEntry."Entry Type"::"Appln. Rounding",
                                    dEntry."Entry Type"::"Correction of Remaining Amount":
                                      BEGIN
                                        mEntryDescription := tRounding;
                                        mEntryDueDate := 0D;
                                      END;
                                  END;

                                  IF (lIncludeEntry) THEN
                                    mEntryBalanceAmount += dEntry.Amount;
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1000000038;1;DataItem;dOverdueEntryCurrency;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 WHERE(Number=FILTER(1..));
               PrintOnlyIfDetail=Yes;
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               mCurrencyTmp.RESET();
                               IF (dCustomer.GETFILTER("Currency Filter") <> '') THEN
                                 dCustomer.COPYFILTER("Currency Filter", mCurrencyTmp.Code);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  lContinue@1000000000 : Boolean;
                                BEGIN
                                  IF (( NOT (mShowOverdueEntries)) AND ( NOT (mIncludeAgingBand))) THEN

                                  IF (dOverdueEntryCurrency.Number = 1) THEN
                                    lContinue := mCurrencyTmp.FINDSET()
                                  ELSE
                                    lContinue := (mCurrencyTmp.NEXT <> 0);
                                  IF ( NOT (lContinue)) THEN
                                    CurrReport.BREAK();

                                  mCustLedgerEntry.RESET();
                                  mCustLedgerEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Customer No.", "Posting Date", "Currency Code");
                                  mCustLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Customer No.", dCustomer."No.");

                                  mCustLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Currency Code", mCurrencyTmp.Code);

    { 9065;2   ;DataItem;dOverdueEntry       ;
               DataItemTable=Table21;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Customer No.,Open,Positive,Due Date);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               CurrReport.CREATETOTALS(dOverdueEntry."Remaining Amount");
                               IF ( NOT (mIncludeAgingBand)) THEN
                                 dOverdueEntry.SETRANGE("Due Date", 0D, mEndDate - 1);
                               dOverdueEntry.SETRANGE("Currency Code", mCurrencyTmp.Code);
                               dOverdueEntry.SETRANGE("Date Filter", 0D, mEndDate);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF (mIncludeAgingBand) THEN
                                    IF ((dOverdueEntry."Posting Date" > mEndDate) AND (dOverdueEntry."Due Date" >= mEndDate)) THEN
                                      CurrReport.SKIP();

                                  dOverdueEntry.CALCFIELDS("Remaining Amount");
                                  IF (dOverdueEntry."Remaining Amount" = 0) THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP();

                                  IF (mIncludeAgingBand) AND (dOverdueEntry."Posting Date" <= mEndDate) THEN
                                    UpdateAgingBandBuffer(mCurrencyTmp.Code, GetDate(dOverdueEntry."Posting Date", dOverdueEntry."Due Date"),
                                      dOverdueEntry."Remaining Amount");

                                  IF (dOverdueEntry."Due Date" >= mEndDate) THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP();
                                END;

               DataItemLinkReference=dCustomer;
               DataItemLink=Customer No.=FIELD(No.) }

                             ENG=Aging Band Date Selection];
                  OptionCaptionML=[ENU=Due Date,Posting Date;
                                   ENG=Due Date,Posting Date];

      { 4   ;2   ;Field     ;
                  Name=LogInteractionField;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetDate@3(pPostingDate@1000 : Date;pDueDate@1001 : Date) : Date;
    BEGIN
      IF (mAgingBandDateSelection = mAgingBandDateSelection::"Posting Date") THEN
        EXIT(pPostingDate)
      ELSE
        EXIT(pDueDate);
    END;

    PROCEDURE SkipReversedUnapplied@4(VAR DtldCustLedgEntries@1000 : Record 379) : Boolean;
    VAR
      CustLedgEntry@1001 : Record 21;
    BEGIN
      IF ((mIncludeReversedEntries) AND (mIncludeUnappliedEntries)) THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      IF ( NOT (mIncludeUnappliedEntries)) THEN
        IF DtldCustLedgEntries.Unapplied THEN
          EXIT(TRUE);
      IF ( NOT (mIncludeReversedEntries)) THEN
      BEGIN
        CustLedgEntry.GET(DtldCustLedgEntries."Cust. Ledger Entry No.");
        IF CustLedgEntry.Reversed THEN
          EXIT(TRUE);
      END;
      EXIT(FALSE);
    END;

    PROCEDURE InitialiseRequestPage@5(pShowOverdueEntries@1000 : Boolean;pIncludeAllCustomersWithEntries@1001 : Boolean;pIncludeAllCustomersWithBalance@1002 : Boolean;pIncludeReversedEntries@1003 : Boolean;pIncludeUnappliedEntries@1004 : Boolean;pIncludeAgingBand@1005 : Boolean;pAgingBandPeriodLengthText@1006 : Text[30];pAgingBandDateSelection@1007 : Option;pLogInteraction@1008 : Boolean;pStartDate@1009 : Date;pEndDate@1010 : Date);
    BEGIN
      InitialiseRequestPageData();

      mShowOverdueEntries := pShowOverdueEntries;
      mIncludeAllCustomersWithEntries := pIncludeAllCustomersWithEntries;
      mIncludeAllCustomersWithBalance := pIncludeAllCustomersWithBalance;
      mIncludeReversedEntries := pIncludeReversedEntries;
      mIncludeUnappliedEntries := pIncludeUnappliedEntries;
      mIncludeAgingBand := pIncludeAgingBand;
      EVALUATE(mAgingBandPeriodLength, pAgingBandPeriodLengthText);
      mAgingBandDateSelection := pAgingBandDateSelection;
      mLogInteraction := pLogInteraction;
      mStartDate := pStartDate;
      mEndDate := pEndDate;
    END;

    PROCEDURE InitialiseRequestPageData@1091();
    VAR
      lEmptyDateFormula@1000000000 : DateFormula;
    BEGIN
      IF (mRequestPageInitialized) THEN
        EXIT;

      IF (( NOT (mIncludeAllCustomersWithEntries)) AND ( NOT (mIncludeAllCustomersWithBalance))) THEN
        mIncludeAllCustomersWithBalance := TRUE;

      IF (mAgingBandPeriodLength = lEmptyDateFormula) THEN
        EVALUATE(mAgingBandPeriodLength, '<1M+CM>');

      mRequestPageInitialized := TRUE;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE InitialiseCurrencies@1000000000();
    VAR
      lCurrency@1000000000 : Record 4;
    BEGIN
      lCurrency.RESET();
      IF (lCurrency.FINDSET()) THEN
      REPEAT
        mCurrencyTmp := lCurrency;
        mCurrencyTmp.INSERT();
      UNTIL (lCurrency.NEXT() = 0);

      IF ( NOT (mCurrencyTmp.GET(''))) THEN
      BEGIN
        CLEAR(mCurrencyTmp);
        mCurrencyTmp.INSERT();
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CalculateAgingBandDates@1();
    VAR
      lEmptyDateFormula@1000000000 : DateFormula;
      eAgingBandEndingDateEmpty@1000000001 : TextConst 'ENU=You must specify Aging Band Ending Date.;ENG=You must specify Aging Band Ending Date.';
      eAgingBandPeriodLengthEmpty@1000000002 : TextConst 'ENU=You must specify the Aging Band Period Length.;ENG=You must specify the Aging Band Period Length.';
      eReverseDateFormula@1000000003 : TextConst '@@@=Negating the period length: %1 is the period length;ENU=-%1;ENG=-%1';
      lReversedAgingBandPeriodLength@1000000004 : DateFormula;
      ePeriodLengthOutOfRange@1000000005 : TextConst 'ENU=Aging band period length is out of range.;ENG=Aging band period length is out of range.';
    BEGIN
      IF ( NOT (mIncludeAgingBand)) THEN
        EXIT;

      IF (mEndDate = 0D) THEN
        ERROR(eAgingBandEndingDateEmpty);
      IF (mAgingBandPeriodLength = lEmptyDateFormula) THEN
        ERROR(eAgingBandPeriodLengthEmpty);

      EVALUATE(lReversedAgingBandPeriodLength, STRSUBSTNO(eReverseDateFormula, mAgingBandPeriodLength));

      mAgingBandDate[5] := mEndDate;
      mAgingBandDate[4] := CALCDATE(lReversedAgingBandPeriodLength, mAgingBandDate[5]);
      mAgingBandDate[3] := CALCDATE(lReversedAgingBandPeriodLength, mAgingBandDate[4]);
      mAgingBandDate[2] := CALCDATE(lReversedAgingBandPeriodLength, mAgingBandDate[3]);
      mAgingBandDate[1] := CALCDATE(lReversedAgingBandPeriodLength, mAgingBandDate[2]);

      IF (mAgingBandDate[2] <= mAgingBandDate[1]) THEN
        ERROR(ePeriodLengthOutOfRange);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdateAgingBandBuffer@2(pCurrencyCode@1000 : Code[10];pDate@1001 : Date;pAmount@1002 : Decimal);
    VAR
      lDateIndex@1003 : Integer;
      lMaxDateIndex@1000000000 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      IF ( NOT (mAgingBandBufferTmp.GET(pCurrencyCode))) THEN
      BEGIN
        CLEAR(mAgingBandBufferTmp);
        mAgingBandBufferTmp.INIT();
        mAgingBandBufferTmp.VALIDATE("Currency Code", pCurrencyCode);
        mAgingBandBufferTmp.INSERT(TRUE);
      END;

      lMaxDateIndex := ARRAYLEN(mAgingBandDate);
      FOR lDateIndex := 1 TO lMaxDateIndex DO
        IF (pDate <= mAgingBandDate[lDateIndex]) THEN
        BEGIN
          AddToAgingBandBuffer(lDateIndex, pAmount);
          lDateIndex := lMaxDateIndex;
        END;

      mAgingBandBufferTmp.MODIFY(TRUE);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE AddToAgingBandBuffer@1000000002(pIndex@1000000001 : Integer;pAmount@1000000000 : Decimal);
    BEGIN
      CASE (pIndex) OF
        1: mAgingBandBufferTmp."Column 1 Amt." += pAmount;
        2: mAgingBandBufferTmp."Column 2 Amt." += pAmount;
        3: mAgingBandBufferTmp."Column 3 Amt." += pAmount;
        4: mAgingBandBufferTmp."Column 4 Amt." += pAmount;
        5: mAgingBandBufferTmp."Column 5 Amt." += pAmount;
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE DecideWhetherToIncludeCustomer@1000000007() : Boolean;
    VAR
      lIncludeCustomer@1000000000 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      lIncludeCustomer := FALSE;

      mCustomer := dCustomer;
      dCustomer.COPYFILTER("Currency Filter", mCurrencyTmp.Code);
      IF (mIncludeAllCustomersWithBalance) THEN
      BEGIN
        mCurrencyTmp.RESET();
        IF (mCurrencyTmp.FINDSET()) THEN
        REPEAT
          mCustomer.SETRANGE("Date Filter", 0D, mEndDate);
          mCustomer.SETRANGE("Currency Filter", mCurrencyTmp.Code);
          mCustomer.CALCFIELDS("Net Change");
          lIncludeCustomer := (mCustomer."Net Change" <> 0);
        UNTIL ((mCurrencyTmp.NEXT() = 0) OR (lIncludeCustomer));
      END;

      IF (( NOT (lIncludeCustomer)) AND (mIncludeAllCustomersWithEntries)) THEN
      BEGIN
        mCustLedgerEntry.RESET();
        mCustLedgerEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Customer No.","Posting Date");
        mCustLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Customer No.", dCustomer."No.");
        mCustLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Posting Date", mStartDate, mEndDate);
        dCustomer.COPYFILTER("Currency Filter", mCustLedgerEntry."Currency Code");
        lIncludeCustomer := ( NOT (mCustLedgerEntry.ISEMPTY));
      END;

      EXIT(lIncludeCustomer);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdateLastStatementNo@1000000003();
    BEGIN
      IF ( NOT (CurrReport.PREVIEW)) THEN
      BEGIN
        dCustomer.LOCKTABLE;
        dCustomer."Last Statement No." += 1;
        dCustomer.MODIFY(TRUE);
        COMMIT();
      END ELSE
        dCustomer."Last Statement No." += 1;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE VerifyDates@7();
    VAR
      lDateBuffer@1000000000 : Date;
      eBlankStartDateErr@1000000002 : TextConst 'ENU=Start Date must have a value.;ENG=Start Date must have a value.';
      eBlankEndDateErr@1000000001 : TextConst 'ENU=End Date must have a value.;ENG=End Date must have a value.';
    BEGIN
      IF (mStartDate = 0D) THEN
        ERROR(eBlankStartDateErr);
      IF (mEndDate = 0D) THEN
        ERROR(eBlankEndDateErr);
      IF (mStartDate > mEndDate) THEN
      BEGIN
        lDateBuffer := mEndDate;
        mEndDate := mStartDate;
        mStartDate := lDateBuffer;
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE DetectLogInteraction@1000000004();
    VAR
      lInteractionLogEntry@1000000000 : Record 5065;
    BEGIN
      mLogInteractionEnabled := (mSegManagement.FindInteractTmplCode(lInteractionLogEntry."Document Type"::"Sales Stmnt.") <> '');
      mLogInteraction := mLogInteractionEnabled;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE LogInteraction@1000000001();
    VAR
      lInteractionLogEntry@1000000001 : Record 5065;
    BEGIN
      IF ( NOT (mLogInteraction)) THEN
        EXIT;
      IF (CurrReport.PREVIEW) THEN
        EXIT;
      mSegManagement.LogDocument(lInteractionLogEntry."Document Type"::"Sales Stmnt.", FORMAT(dCustomer."Last Statement No."),
        0, 0, DATABASE::Customer, dCustomer."No.", dCustomer."Salesperson Code", '',
        STRSUBSTNO(tStatementTitle, dCustomer."Last Statement No."), '');
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CurrencyCode@1000000008(pCurrencyCode@1000000000 : Code[10]) : Code[10];
    BEGIN
      IF (pCurrencyCode <> '') THEN
        EXIT(pCurrencyCode)
      ELSE
        EXIT(mGeneralLedgerSetup."LCY Code");
    END;

    BEGIN

      //DOC NH2016.4  JH 23/09/2015 - Upgraded to 2016
      //DOC NH2016.15 JH 10/05/2016 - CfMD amendments
    }
    END.

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
